# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 22:09:26.163097

### Base Program

```py
def broken_calc(startValue: int, target: int) -> int:
    operations = 0
    while target > startValue:
        target = target // 2 if target % 2 == 0 else target + 1
        operations += 1
    return operations + startValue - target
```

### Input

```json
[19, 32]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def broken_calc(startValue: int, target: int) -> int:
    operations = 0
    while target > startValue:
        target = target // 2 if target % 2 == 0 else target + 1
        operations += 1
    return operations + startValue - target
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def broken_calc(var_0: int, var_1: int) -> int:
    operations = 0
    while var_1 > var_0:
        var_1 = var_1 // 2 if var_1 % 2 == 0 else var_1 + 1
        operations += 1
    return operations + var_0 - var_1
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def broken_calc(startValue: int, target: int) -> int:
    operations = 0
    while target > startValue:
        target = target // 2 if target % 2 == 0 else 1 + target
        operations += 1
    return startValue + operations + -target
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def broken_calc(var_2: int, var_3: int) -> int:
    operations = 0
    while var_3 > var_2:
        var_3 = var_3 // 2 if var_3 % 2 == 0 else 1 + var_3
        operations += 1
    return var_2 + operations + -var_3
```
